After thinking for a moment, Song Shuhang looked at Senior White’s clone, Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue, and Senior Spirit Butterfly. “Seniors, are you fine with this?”

While most of the (Braised Heavenly Tribulation) was made by him, he did get some help from these seniors. Therefore, Song Shuhang wanted to consult them before confirming the transaction.

Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue smiled. “This (Braised Heavenly Tribulation) was made by you, and we only lent you a hand. Having said that, you can decide on this kind of thing yourself.”

“If you want to trade with them, then go ahead,” Senior White’s clone said. “Anyway, we can always make more.”

They still had a lot of raw ingredients, enough for a whole banquet for the Nine Provinces Number One Group and more.

“Thank you, Seniors.” Song Shuhang hoisted up the first completed (Braised Heavenly Tribulation) and said, “Then, please, Senior Shadow, try my Braised Heavenly Tribulation and tell me if it passes!”

In the half of Heavenly Field Island that was shrouded in darkness, a pair of small arms condensed, extending by 200 meters. They took the Braised Heavenly Tribulation from Song Shuhang and brought it back into the darkness.

The completed Braised Heavenly Tribulation was a plain red with a dark-golden aura around it, along with a rich, lasting fragrance that made people drool.

Soon after, a soft chewing sound came from the darkness.

Lord Shadow exclaimed, “Delicious! It’s just like how I remember it. When you take a bite, the first layer is fat but not greasy, and it melts in your mouth. The second layer is chewy, and the more you eat, the more fragrant it gets. Then the third layer is extremely crunchy and easily breaks apart when you bite into it. Moreover, this is even more fragrant and tasty than the Braised Heavenly Tribulation I remember.”

“!!!” Song Shuhang.

Lord Shadow has eaten the Braised Heavenly Tribulation in the past? Doesn’t that mean that... he knows Demon Emperor Hezhi?

If so, should I stab him while he’s eating?

As soon as this thought emerged in his mind, Song Shuhang kicked it in the depths of his mind.

Going against big shots wasn’t something he should turn into a hobby.

In fact, every time he ended up having to fight against a big shot, it was a matter of coincidence, and sometimes it was the big shot who was inexplicably making trouble for him. He had rarely taken the initiative to attack them. Regarding this matter which greatly concerned his life, he was still clear of mind.

Moreover, merely knowing Demon Emperor Hezhi did not necessarily mean they were friends. There was a possibility that Senior Shadow had just been a guest of Demon Emperor Hezhi.

I shouldn’t make Senior Shadow my enemy just because he had had a taste of Demon Emperor Hezhi’s Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet.

(I have a grudge with the owner of the steamed bun store next door, so anyone who has eaten his steamed buns is also my enemy.) This logic was simply flawed.

Furthermore... Senior Shadow was a customer introduced by the Almighty Merchant. If he were to provoke Senior Shadow, he would definitely be blacklisted by the Almighty Merchant.

He had just regained his chance to trade with the other party, so he shouldn’t lose sight of the bigger picture.

And so, Song Shuhang quickly put away the thought of stabbing Senior Shadow.

At this moment, Lord Shadow spoke once again. “Little Fellow Daoist, have you improved the recipe for the Braised Heavenly Tribulation?”

Song Shuhang nodded. “It can’t really be said to be an improvement, more like an accident. We accidentally added a Big Dipper to the mix while making the dish. And besides that, in order to make the ingredients more delicious, I tried using a secret technique.” “This dish is really not bad. If I were to rate your Braised Heavenly Tribulation, I would give you an 80 out of 100. While your cooking skills might be far inferior to that other cook, causing the taste of the dish to be affected, adding the Big Dipper to the dish and your improvement of the ingredients gave it a lot of points,” Lord Shadow praised. “This Braised Heavenly Tribulation passed the test. However, little Fellow Daoist, there is still much room for improvement in your immortal cooking skills. I hope that you’re able to create a dish that merits 95 points from me in the future. I will tell you this now as I’m quite the picky eater.”

“Thank you for your compliment, Senior.” Song Shuhang smiled slightly.

This was the first time he had even tried immortal cooking, and he had already gotten recognized by a senior. Perhaps he actually had a lot of talent in this regard?

Lord Shadow asked, “Since the dish was up to standard, our transaction is complete. So, little friend, is there anything you want?” While Lord Shadow spoke to him, Song Shuhang felt a kind of ‘air’ blow toward his face.

[No need to be shy. Go ahead and tell me what you want. Even if you desire the stars in the sky, I can easily pluck them down for you! As long as it is what you want, I will satisfy your wish.] The virtuous lamia raised her head and spoke using a magnetic male voice, reciting the lines from a TV show.

Fairy Creation clapped her hands in response.

“...” Song Shuhang.

The atmosphere was suddenly destroyed.

Senior Shadow laughed. “Hahaha, if you want stars, then I can indeed give them to you.”

Song Shuhang waved his hands repeatedly in response, indicating his refusal.

What would I do with stars? It’s not like I can stuff them into my Inner World.

And one day, if my Inner World were to actually grow large enough to house stars, then I would be able to pluck them down myself.

Song Shuhang said, “Please wait, Senior. In fact, there is something that I want.”

After that, he turned to look at Senior Turtle and whispered, “Senior Turtle, do you know of the Eastern Spring Pavilion?”

Senior Turtle responded, “Heavens, you aren’t even going to spare the Great Eastern Emperor?”

Shuhang had already taken the Great Southern Emperor’s old home, and now he was going to go for the Great Eastern Emperor’s?

“So it really is the Great Eastern Emperor’s palace.” Song Shuhang nodded silently.

Mm-hm, that’s it!

Song Shuhang said, “Senior, can I ask for some fragments of the Ancient Heavenly City’s Eastern Spring Pavilion?”

“!!!” Fairy Almighty Seller glared at Song Shuhang. “I’ll blacklist you, Customer Song!”

“Fairy, don’t get me wrong. I don’t mean to target the Eastern Spring Pavilion’s fragments that you have. I was thinking that since the pavilion was shattered, there should be a lot of fragments. What you want to collect and sell is only a few of them; I’ll settle for the others,” Song Shuhang explained.

Fairy Almighty Seller squeezed her chin and nodded. “That makes sense.”

“Fragments of the Eastern Spring Pavilion? Got it.” Senior Shadow nodded slightly.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior, you have fragments on you?” “No, today’s actually the first time I’ve heard of such a thing. But it’s fine, because I’m rich,” said Senior Shadow.

“...” Song Shuhang.

After Senior Shadow finished speaking, he said to the Almighty Merchant, “Fellow Daoist, I want to buy a few fragments of the Eastern Spring Pavilion. At that time, I’ll settle the bill together with the request for the Braised Heavenly Tribulation, what do you think?” “Sure.” The Almighty Merchant displayed a sincere smile-he liked this kind of customer the most, the kind that never bargained. As long as the transaction was completed, no matter how many spirit stones it cost, the other party would generously settle the cost.

Fairy Almighty Seller said, “Master, don’t take the fragments I’m going for!”

The Almighty Merchant patted his disciple’s head lightly and smiled. “Today, Master will teach you another lesson. There is competition in business.”

“!!!” Fairy Almighty Seller exclaimed, “I want to dissolve our master-disciple relationship!”

Smiling, the Almighty Merchant said, “It’s merely a master-disciple relationship, how can that even come close to comparing to business?”

“...” Song Shuhang.

It seems that spirit stones can not only buy the smiles of a Tribulation Transcender and an Immortal, but also make them turn against each other.

Fairy Almighty Seller stomped angrily.

The Almighty Merchant lightly patted her head again. “I’m just kidding. Regarding the fragments of the Eastern Spring Pavilion, I still have many channels that I can use. You go ahead and complete your own transaction.” “Then, the deal is done,” said Senior Shadow with a smile. Afterward, his huge body began to retreat into the spatial gate.

Before going back, he suddenly threw a black cup at Song Shuhang. “With that cup, you can summon me once. In the future, when you’ve better learned the Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet dishes, you can summon me. As long as your dishes are up to standard, I will reward you. Is the next dish going to be (Smoked Inner Demon Tribulation Slices)?”

The black-skinned Soft Feather suddenly felt chills all over her body.

Song Shuhang accepted the small black cup and replied, “I haven’t really thought of that yet. In fact, I learned about the Heavenly Tribulation Menu not too long ago.”

“Hahaha! I’m looking forward to our next meeting.” Senior Shadow laughed heartily as he retreated to the Shadow Realm, disappearing without a trace.

After Senior Shadow left, Heavenly Field Island returned to its original state.

The banquet that belonged to the Nine Provinces Number One Group had officially started.

With Senior Shadow’s acknowledgment, Song Shuhang began to cook the remaining Third Stage tribulation lightning strips into Braised Lightning Tribulations.

The Almighty Merchant and Fairy Almighty Seller, who were forced by Song Shuhang to stay, also attended the banquet.

Those who eat one’s food become much more amenable to one’s requests. As long as they attend this banquet, while I might not get much of a discount the next time I want to buy something from the Almighty Merchant, it should at least be a lot easier to find him, right? Song Shuhang thought to himself.

The Braised Heavenly Tribulation, Lady Kuna’s immortal brew, and the immortal tea from that mysterious young senior. Each was an exceedingly rare treasure. After three rounds of drinking... the Almighty Merchant began to bring out the immortal dishes he had preserved in his private space. These immortal dishes were of all kinds of age, and there was a large variety of them. Since these dishes were stored by the Almighty Merchant, they were guaranteed to be no worse than any dish made by Immortal Fairy Bie Xue.

What was originally only a Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet had now become a feast no worse than the Immortal Feast.

The banquet lasted deep into the night! The members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, who had already been drinking a lot, drank even more.

Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly tightly held a piece of Braised Heavenly Tribulation, savoring its taste as he ate it.

In addition to the three different experiences that came with each bite as Senior Shadow had stated, the Braised Heavenly Tribulation also came with an explosive taste when swallowed. This was the original taste of the heavenly tribulation!

After having lived for so many years, I’ve finally come to know what the heavenly tribulation tastes like.

As he thought of this, Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly toasted with Venerable Yellow Mountain.

This wine is also wonderful. It must be a treasure of the Ninth Stage rank or higher.

It’s truly quite unexpected that little friend Shuhang was able to gather so many great things. It looks like he’s also a guy with special luck.

Compared with Fellow Daoist White’s luck, Song Shuhang’s luck should be a display of ‘fate’.

“Eh? Have I drunk too much?” Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly suddenly murmured to himself.

He felt like he was seeing things.

When he had glanced over just now, he saw that there were three Soft Feathers.

The black-skinned Soft Feather sat beside him obediently, and he saw two other Soft Feathers walking through the crowd at the banquet, rolling around and laughing.

“Mm-hm, it seems that I really have drunk too much.” Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly smiled. He was a handsome middle-aged man, so after smiling, his charm only grew higher, and he could only be said to be absolutely stunning.

Some of the young girls on Heavenly Field Island were stunned silly as they saw his smile.

“Senior Song, Senior Song!” At this moment, the Soft Feather wrapped in a sheet rolled in front of Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “What is it, Soft Feather?”

Soft Feather giggled, rolled over to Sixteen next to Shuhang, and then lay her head on Sixteen’s lap before saying, “I still want to watch a meteor shower.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

I really don’t know what to tell you besides that I’m not omnipotent, Soft Feather.

While he was in thought, Song Shuhang’s eyes suddenly lit up.

“That’s right.” He looked at the Almighty Merchant next to him and said, “Senior, can I buy a meteor shower and use the Braised Heavenly Tribulation to pay for it?”

The Almighty Merchant said boldly, “Hahaha! You don’t need to pay me anything. I’m in a great mood today, so I’ll give you one for free!”

When Fairy Almighty Seller heard this, she knew that her master had absolutely drunk too much.

It was only when he was drunk that her master would not mind giving away small things for free.

“How do you want the meteor shower to look?” While saying this, the Almighty Merchant stood up and directed his hands at the sky.

At this moment... In the sky, a meteor shower appeared, shining as it descended. It was beautiful.

In the next moment, Song Shuhang saw a beautiful meteor shower appear in the sky. The meteors streaked across the night sky, littering it with beautiful streaks of light. It was an absolutely stunning scene.

It was as if a god had smashed a star apart specifically to create a meteor shower.

“So beautiful- It’s a lot more beautiful than what I imagined,” Soft Feather said with great satisfaction. She rested her head on Sixteen’s knee, and looked up at the starry sky with a satisfied look on her face. “Thank you, Senior Song. Thank you, Senior Almighty Merchant.”

“I...” The Almighty Merchant had his hands raised stiffly, still accumulating power. Then after a while, he squeezed out a sentence. “F*ck, someone stole my business!”

“???” Song Shuhang.

“Huh?” Fairy Almighty Seller looked at her master in surprise. This was the first time that she’d seen her master having his business stolen from him!

“I’m not the one who made this meteor shower.” The Almighty Merchant felt a stifled feeling in his heart.

For the first time in his life, just as he was about to complete a transaction, someone stole the job from him. Although he was giving away this meteor shower for free, he still considered gifting things a kind of transaction!

“Then, who made this meteor shower?” Song Shuhang asked curiously. He turned his head to look at Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly. If the meteor shower wasn’t made by the Almighty Merchant, the next most likely person to do this kind of thing was Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly.

As he turned to look at Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly, he saw the other party holding a glass of wine in his hand, taking small sips from it with a charming smile that made the hearts of the young girls in the surroundings beat wildly. It shouldn’t be Senior Spirit Butterfly, right? He’s too drunk to do such a thing.

Then, who was it? Song Shuhang thought to himself.

At this moment, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword’s scabbard said, “It might be... because of us?”

Song Shuhang responded, “What?”

“Scarlet Heaven and the Great Southern Emperor are fighting, and the meteor shower __ 11

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword suddenly had to stop talking

Young Master Phoenix Slayer, that is simply too frightening of a possibility to even think of.

Doudou is engaged again? He’s going to get married once more?

Those with this disorder would choose to escape from their marriage or hope that their companions would also get married so that they can face what they deem horrors of marriage with their companions. Some others hope that their companions naturally bring up the topic of ‘marriage’ so that they could discuss it thoroughly and seek some comfort through the discussion. I feel that Doudou was trying to rope Song Shuhang into a discussion on marriage by talking about his daughter. Unfortunately for him, the discussion was interrupted midway.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

Meanwhile, outside Heavenly Field Island.

The Almighty Merchant had finished his call, and he had agreed on the location of the delivery with the person on the other side of the call.

When he ended the call, he turned his head and saw ‘Soft Feather’.

Chapter 1865 Rich lady falling in love with a poor young man

The Almighty Merchant recalled that this little fairy was Sage Monarch Butterfly’s only daughter, a potential VIP client. Although her current strength wasn’t that high, her luck was exceptional. Coupled with her outspoken personality, she was definitely someone he could enlist into the ‘buy, buy, buy’ army in the future.

Compared with Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, who was only suitable for selling ‘resurrection magical treasures’ to, the future prospects of this little fairy Soft Feather were much greater.

Frankly, in terms of purchasing power, male cultivators really couldn’t compare with fairies. It was a lot more difficult to get spirit stones from male cultivators than from fairies.

This was the experience that Almighty Merchant had had over the past thousands of years... No matter how the times had changed, fairies would always be much more willing to spend money than male cultivators.

But why did this fairy of Spirit Butterfly Island run here?

While he was in thought, Fairy Soft Feather’s eyes met his. At that moment, she showed a happy smile on her face, and waved at him excitedly. “Senior Almighty Merchant, I finally found you.”

Could it be that there’s something that Fairy Soft Feather wants to buy from me?

As he thought of this, the Almighty Merchant showed a gentle professional smile, and said, “Fairy Soft Feather, is there anything you want to buy?”

The Eastern Spring Pavilion was given to Song Shuhang as a reward by Senior Shadow for the Braised Heavenly Tribulation. That little fellow Tyrannical Song is currently penniless, and he had to borrow money from Sage Monarch White. And now, even this Fairy Soft Feather is quietly paying for him?

Oh yeah, Senior, don’t say that I paid for it, okay?” “Hahaha, of course, we always heed our customers’ requests.” The Almighty Merchant gave her a thumbs-up, and then said, “By the way, Fairy Soft Feather, it’s fine if you don’t answer this, but I’ve been wanting to know, do you like Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song?”

Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, whose pockets were even emptier than those of a homeless man, was liked by such a beautiful and rich fairy.

The Almighty Merchant truly did not expect that he would encounter the plot of a ‘rich lady falling in love with a poor young man’ in the main world.

The Almighty Merchant said, “I’ll be there shortly.”

Where did he go?

Could it be that the group of drunks at the banquet hadn’t eaten enough, and they still wanted more food?

(Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s steel manifestation. This manifestation is a special clone of Profound Sage Tyrannical Song that he refined at the Fifth Stage. It is closely related to his Spirit Lake, and it is an integral part of Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.]

Chapter 1866 Seven-day return service

After a long while, she remembered what she had forgotten to do. “Ah, right, I forgot to get in touch with that little girl Soft Feather.” The Heavenly Emperor looked up at the sky-her main purpose this time was obviously to get in touch with Soft Feather to find out what the latter was doing recently. The Heavenly Emperor really didn’t like the sudden bursts of comfort that she would experience every now and then.

At the banquet on Heavenly Field Island. Most of the fellow daoists who were already too drunk were sent to rest under the arrangement of Island Master Tian Tiankong. There were a few others who were still barely awake, and had yet to fall asleep.

You guys are really evenly matched. One of you had your ghost spirit taken away by the Heavenly Emperor, while the other had their steel manifestation taken away by the Heavenly Emperor. Motherf*cker...

In this world filled with cruel and cunning people, only the sheet wrapped around his body could bring him warmth.

Seven-day return service: no matter where you are, as long as you are unsatisfied with the goods, we can immediately come and pick up the goods for you. Excellent service all for you!

Chapter 1867 I feel like the seniors really like the concept of seven days

In order to keep up with the times, the Almighty Merchant had been preparing to launch a seven-day return service for all his customers.

However, he had yet to plan everything out and perfect the related magical techniques. In short, he had not formally introduced this service to his customers just yet.

He could use the goods as the coordinates to carry out the pickup service at any time. The three Eastern Spring Pavilion Fragments that were taken away by the Heavenly Emperor also had this seven-day return service function!

do.”

After recovering the Eastern Spring Pavilion Fragments and completing the transaction with Song Shuhang, he had decided that he was really going to blacklist him, and never remove him from the list again.

This guy is a huge pitfall, an abyss! I thought that I was not going to fall into a pit this time, but look where I’m now.

But I really am also innocent here.

This time, I’ve really made a big loss.”

However, he could not deny that the wine tasted amazing

I wonder where Tyrannical Song got that wine from... There shouldn’t be a lot of immortal brew at that level across the universe, right?

Should I buy some from him in the future?

Take a step back! I can’t let there be a next time.

Master seems to be having a lot of internal conflicts today... Could he be experiencing menopause? Or, is he experiencing a ‘great aunt’?

The ‘great aunt[1]’ was actually a commodity, and it was quite a popular one in the universe.

People were always sentimental, and they came to miss what they had lost. Therefore, there were some powerful fairy maidens who would feel reminiscent of old times, and wanted to experience what it was like to menstruate once more.

I’m really going to try looking for a customer tomorrow and see how much I can sell Almighty Seller for.

Back on Heavenly Field Island.

Chapter 1868 My loli voice

The inner demon clone, as its name suggested, was a manifestation of one’s own inner demon that turned into a clone.

The inner demon, which was feared by most cultivators, was completely changed by Soft Feather. This one magical technique of hers completely transformed how the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group saw the inner demons. Of course, Soft Feather’s inner demon being so well-behaved was a special case. The members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group all knew that Soft Feather’s brain was simply wired differently from those of normal cultivators. She was currently the only member who was not afraid of Senior White’s punishments, and even felt they were very exciting.

Therefore, everyone was curious about what kind of inner demon clone Northern River’s Loose Cultivator would condense.

Were all inner demon clones special? Or was it just Soft Feather’s inner demon clone that was weird?

And finally, was the inner demon clone magical technique worth promoting to the rest of the members of the group?

Moreover, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword had also managed to condense an ‘inner demon clone’.

Song Shuhang looked at Soft Feather and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, and said, “This is the first time I’ve heard of a divine weapon having an inner demon.”

After a divine weapon gained consciousness, an artifact spirit was born.

Unlike humans, artifact spirits had pure consciousness bodies, so in theory, they shouldn’t have something like an ‘inner demon’.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword laughed, and said, “Haha! I, Scarlet Heaven Sword, am different. After all, I am an Immortal’s divine weapon.”

Inner demons were all-encompassing. Anything imaginable could become an inner demon. Song Shuhang was very curious: since Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword was a sword, then what kind of ‘desire’ or ‘psychological flaw’ did the other party have?

The puppet maiden sat next to Song Shuhang in the same posture. Her orange eyes shone like lights on Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword as she said in a mechanical voice, “Senior is a treasured sword, but it can use both saber intent and saber qi. As such, I boldly speculate that this is Senior’s inner demon!”

She always felt that Song Shuhang’s style would suddenly change whenever Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword was present. It was like he would be suddenly possessed by Senior Thrice Reckless.

To be precise, it should be because of the influence of my inner demon on him.” ...If it weren’t for that, it would have already unsheathed itself and stabbed Song Shuhang’s waist. How could it possibly still be sitting there and letting its heart be rent? After saying that, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword lightly touched the ground with its tip.

From its shadow, a figure slowly emerged. Similar to Soft Feather’s inner demon clone, its inner demon clone also emerged from the shadows.

The first thing that appeared was its hilt.

It was a very normal-looking hilt. It bore the same style as Scarlet Heaven Sword, just that it was colored black.

“...” Su Clan’s Sixteen.

What appeared after the hilt was not the body of the sword, but rather very well-built pectoral muscles.

After that came well-toned abs.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “By the way, are we really inner demons?”

If they were inner demons, then why were they protecting Song Shuhang and the others? Normally speaking, shouldn’t an inner demon stand by the side and watch everyone die?

I feel like you and I are fake inner demons.

“Butterfly-Eagle Transformation!” The black-skinned Soft Feather did not bother with any nonsense. As she swung the sword, sword qi in the form of an eagle with butterfly wings on its back shot toward the floating skull.

Clang!

Behind her, a pair of hands quietly returned to Song Shuhang’s chest—these hands belonged to his ghost spirit.

Song Shuhang’s ghost spirit had not been affected by the ‘time stop’. If the black-skinned Soft Feather had not been able to block the skull just now, it would have taken her place in defending Song Shuhang.

“This is bad. That skull is too strong for me,” the black-skinned Soft Feather said. “Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, aren’t you an Immortal’s divine weapon? Logically speaking, you should be very sharp, right? Why can’t you cut that skull apart?”

I don’t have a corresponding physical body, so how can I be sharp?” the black Scarlet Heaven Sword replied calmly. “Moreover, because of Dharma King Creation’s singing just now, I was greatly weakened. The fact that I’m able to fight alongside you is already exceptional.”

This black Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword is so unreliable.

It was greatly limited due to having traversed time and space. Besides that, maintaining the time ‘frozen’ was also quite costly. This caused it to feel both anxious and enraged at the repeated setbacks that it had suffered.

At this time, cracks were appearing on the skull due to it being unable to handle the force that came with the descent of the will. The energy from the frenzied will spread throughout the skull, merging to form a tentacled creature made of pure energy.

Now, I have to move this tentacle monster away from here. Song Shuhang finely adjusted his position while coming up with several plans in his mind to lure the monster away.

Aggroing monsters was also a kind of skill.

While Song Shuhang was in the middle of thinking... a sharp tentacle suddenly emerged from the space behind him, shooting toward his waist.

Chirk!

His (Variant Steel Hands Technique), (Scholarly Indestructible Body of the Buddha), (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique), Spirit Lake Protective Force Field, light of virtue, golden armor of the Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure, and many other defensive measures had instantly popped out from his body, greatly reducing the damage he had taken.

Perhaps we’ll meet againin the future. Should I try remembering its features so that I can properly say hi the next time we meet? Also... Song Shuhang had always thought that the giant turtles of disaster were some sort of half-mechanical, half-biological creatureslike the big-eyed planet. Chapter 1879 Dawn arrives, darkness leaves

I wonder if the Almighty Merchant is interested in it... It might sell for a pretty good price.

Creatures with spatial abilities were particularly difficult to seal. If one was not careful, they could use their spatial abilities to escape.

It suits little friend Shuhang’s attributes quite well.” Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue nodded, and then said, “However, the heavenly tribulation alone is far from enough. This won’t be able to fully display your fire and lightning dual-attribute talent. There’s still a lot of room for improvement in your illusory reality.”

Venerable Yellow Mountain said, “However, at least a prototype has already been constructed.”

Modifying a prototype was much easier than creating it.

Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly suggested, “Little friend Song can consider improving on the desert. In fact, a desert also hides the attribute of fire. As long as you increase the heat of the desert, you can directly create flames in it. The illusory reality, which is a manifestation of the thoughts and will of a cultivator, can go beyond common sense.” An illusory reality could become however complex one could make it-of course, more complex did not necessarily mean greater lethality and strength. The strength of an illusory reality depended on the depth of one’s spiritual energy, the strength of one’s divine sense, and the cultivator’s realm.

“That is to say, even things that defy the laws of physics could become reality inside an illusory reality?” Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

“Exactly,” said Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly. Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue said, “Improving one’s illusory reality is not a matter that can be done in just a day or two. Moreover, while making use of Fellow Daoist White’s illusory reality as a frame is quite showy, it still isn’t yours in the end. It would do you well to mentally prepare yourself.”

“Thank you, Seniors.” Song Shuhang nodded, and said, “So how do I cancel the illusory reality? After I cancel it, will it still look the same the next time I release it?”

Senior White’s clone said calmly, “The illusory reality is the embodiment of the cultivator’s thoughts. Therefore, as long as you store away those thoughts, it will naturally disappear as

well.”

As if it was an item being stored into a box, the illusory reality World receded to the ground, revealing the 99 demonic god pillars that were acting as its foundation.

The 99 demonic god pillars then merged into Song Shuhang’s shadow and disappeared.

Senior White’s clone analyzed, “Mm-hm, that’s because your current illusory reality is formed by relying on these 99 demonic god pillars. It is not a result of your own strength.”

The 99 demonic god pillars could be regarded as a special magical treasure that could allow Song Shuhang’s thoughts to extend and affect the real world, thus allowing him to achieve the same effect that an illusory reality had.

Soft Feather asked, “Can Senior Song still release the illusory reality after storing it away?”

“Let me try it out.” Song Shuhang closed his eyes, and tried releasing the illusory reality again.

look?”

These puppet clones had no combat power, and only had the ability to link with the user’s five senses. Its main purpose was to be used in place of the user to explore dangerous places. When using these puppet clones, the user would have to devote their whole consciousness to controlling it. One could not multitask while using these puppet clones.

Senior White’s clone handed out a puppet clone to each of the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group. Anyway, these were just products of his experiments from a long time ago. Before this, they were merely wasting away in warehouses.

Song Shuhang also got a puppet clone.

The members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group all activated the puppet clones in their hands-of course, except for Song Shuhang

A golden desert appeared in front of everyone.

At the same time, everyone could feel their own puppet clones replacing the white horse.

This was beyond all of their expectations. They thought that after they entered this illusory reality, they would become either Little White or the young man in green robes!

Song Shuhang’s illusory reality could not separate everyone into their own scenes like Senior White’s illusion. As such, all of the puppet clones were stuffed into a single scene.

The originally dashing arrival of the young man had been downgraded, giving it a shoddy salesman aura.

We didn’t scream yet, so why is little friend Shuhang screaming?

Just now, while he was watching the young man in green robes riding a white horse in the illusory reality and being about to be killed by the Heavenly Tribulation Fire-Lightning Palm, the power of the heavenly tribulation in the illusion was suddenly blocked.

Immediately afterward, Song Shuhang felt like a rocket had been inserted into his body, and he began soaring into the sky... And then he plunged into the Netherworld right after that.

The speed of the ascent and descent was so exhilarating that words simply could not describe the experience—it was hundreds of times more exhilarating than bungee jumping.

This was the first time that he entered the Netherworld Realm in such a way. In the past, he would always use the Inner World as a springboard to enter it, or directly enter it through a spatial gate.

Under the influence of this magical technique, Song Shuhang’s body recovered from a ‘young boy’ to a ‘young man’ in the blink of an eye. This aging technique did not harm his lifespan in the slightest. It simply affected his appearance. From start to finish, Senior White Two did not say a word to him.

The (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique) practiced by Song Shuhang was incomplete. He only had the parts of it until the fifth level. Profound Sage Tyrannical Song really is quite dirty!

Netherworld Evil Energy Infection + Ruler of the Netherworld + Solution.

This method is really dirty!

The ruler of the Netherworld infects the Beast Realm with evil energy, and then Profound Sage Tyrannical Song comes forward to solve the problem. However, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song and the ruler of the Netherworld are actually working together.

For cultivation techniques of this level, the last chapters were usually of the kind that could only be comprehended directly, and not imparted. The cultivation techniques themselves would carry the power of laws, and thus couldn’t simply be copied down with pen and paper. Even if it were forcibly recorded or copied, the written words would be erased by the power of heaven and earth.

Therefore, in order to maintain their integrity, cultivation techniques of this level had special inheritance locations where the future generations could enter to understand the core part. The core part of the (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique), for example, was located in an inheritance location in the Beast Realm.

The (Scholarly Indestructible Body of the Buddha) that Song Shuhang had was also a body-tempering cultivation technique of this level. Luckily, he obtained the complete inheritance directly from the Scholarly Sage’s memory through the Still Pond of Wisdom back at the Mountain of Myriad Books. Otherwise, if he wanted to learn the complete (Scholarly Indestructible Body of the Buddha), he would have to comprehend it from the scholarly faction’s inheritance location.

Sage Monarch Blue Phoenix replied, “Fellow Daoist, you can find the final content of the (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique) in its inheritance location, Garre’s Holy Mountain, which is in the Beast Realm. However, I won’t be able to guarantee whether you will be able to comprehend it.”

“Sure, it’s settled then,” replied Song Shuhang. He was only at the early stages of the Sixth Stage Realm, so even if the version that Fairy Blue Phoenix gave him was inferior to the final content, it should be enough for him to reach the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Realm. That should last him for quite a while, so he was in no hurry at all.

In addition, Song Shuhang was very much... not confident in having the ability to comprehend the final content of the (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique) at Garre’s Holy Mountain.

He recalled when he was in the secret room of the Chu Family, looking at a picture while trying to comprehend the sword art.

Back then, everyone around him was able to comprehend some sword arts or sword moves from the picture, but he could not understand the slightest bit of it.

Fortunately, Song Shuhang was now armed with the secret appraisal technique. He hoped that the inheritance at Garre’s Holy Mountain could be deciphered by the secret appraisal technique and that he would not have to bleed too much.

Fairy Blue Phoenix suggested, “Great. Then, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, how about we meet up in the Jiangnan area of Earth’s China? We’re both familiar with the place, so it should be a good location to meet up at.”

It would take some time to rush back to the Jiangnan area from where he was by flying on a saber, but with Senior White’s clone by his side, he could reach the place with a single spatial jump.

I remember that the inheritance you wanted to set up for Scarlet Pupil isn’t complete yet. And there’s still Senior Eternal Fire of the scholarly faction. When are you making a trip there?”

His clone was stuck in the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation Realm; his steel manifestation was in the hands of the Heavenly Emperor; and his inner demon clone refused to materialize.

There were many things he had to deal with, but he could only do them one at a time.

“!!!” Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly.

He hadn’t noticed previously that his black-skinned daughter had actually been living in the shadow of little friend Song Shuhang

That was to say, his black-skinned daughter would not be returning with him to Spirit Butterfly Island, and would instead go on an adventure with little friend Song Shuhang...

He had originally been thinking of enjoying his time together with his two daughters by his side.

– I want to advance to the Sixth Stage Realm as soon as possible!”

Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly smiled slightlyit was rare that his daughter would take initiative to practice. “In a while, when the fellow daoists wake up, we can say our goodbyes and leave.”

With his daughter taking the initiative to cultivate, he ignored the fact that his black-skinned daughter was being taken away on adventures by Song Shuhang.

On Heavenly Field Island, the hungover cultivators who were struck by Dharma King Creation’s singing woke up one by one.

Chapter 1892 Putting into practice what one has learned

Song Shuhang was taken aback. “What saber technique?”

Fairy Almighty Seller replied, “The (Inverted Scale Saber Technique).”

“...” Song Shuhang.

He had not been expecting it to be this saber technique, so he thought that he had heard wrong at first.

The (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) was the first good saber technique that Song Shuhang had learned in the truest sense. He had mastered the first three styles of this technique, namely the (Dragon Dance Style), the (Dragon Scale Style), and the (Inverted Scale Style).

The saber would move like a dragon, and no evil would be able to invade one’s body. The technique could form scales and protect against threats from all directions. Inverted scale saber intent, the strongest defensive saber!

However, despite the domineering names of the styles, it was actually a defensive saber technique that was the complete opposite of a domineering saber technique.

With the improvement in Song Shuhang’s strength, this saber technique had gradually become unable to keep up with his pace due to its low grade.

Wait... Maybe it’s just the same name?

The world is so big. It’s normal for one or two saber techniques to have the same name.

Song Shuhang asked, “Fairy, is there anything special about this (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) that you just mentioned?”

“It’s good that you asked.” Fairy Almighty Seller reached out, brought out a tablet, and swiped on it a few times. She then said, “It’s a rare and unique cultivation technique. This saber technique is completely different from what’s popular, and its creator was even lauded by my master as a truly talented sabersman.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

Fairy Almighty Seller exclaimed, “This is a saber technique that focuses on defense. You probably can’t even imagine just how powerful this defensive saber technique actually is!”

Song Shuhang stretched out his hand. “Fairy,

wait.”

He got up and shook his right hand. The treasured saber Broken Tyrant emerged from the Inner World, falling into his hand.

Song Shuhang then shook the treasured saber, and the guardrails on it transformed into barbed spikes. If this saber were stabbed into a person’s body, not to mention the pain, the spikes alone would be able to claim their life.

Fairy Almighty Seller looked at Song Shuhang curiously, not knowing what he was planning on doing.

“First, Dragon Dance Style!” Song Shuhang waved Broken Tyrant, and saber qi erupted from it. The qi that condensed did not dissipate, and it instead transformed into a dragon that flew around Song Shuhang.

When the (Dragon Dance Style) was cast, his saber intent armor was also activated.

The saber intent then fused with the saber qi dragon that was flying around him, merging into a beautiful set of armor on Song Shuhang’s body. The entire process of the transformation looked magnificent.

Besides the rather strange fact that the saber intent was armor, everything else was perfect. Whether it was the defensive properties, the counter-attack properties, or the aesthetic, it was all perfect.

“This is the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) evolved version, saber intent armor. Fairy, would you like to learn about it? It’s quite cool.” Song Shuhang gave a thumbs-up.

“...Is that really saber intent? Not armor intent?” Fairy Almighty Seller asked.

“It’s genuine saber intent. As long as you carefully sense it, you’ll be able to see that it’s really saber intent.” Song Shuhang patted the exquisite armor on his body, and said, “Also, its defensive capabilities are top-notch. It won’t lose out even to armor intent.”

“...” Fairy Almighty Seller.

Are you rending my heart on purpose? I just wanted to sell you the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique), yet you go and display an evolved version of it with your saber intent? How am I supposed to do business like this?

SUCC

In the end, Fairy Almighty Seller still successfully completed the transaction of the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) with Song Shuhang in exchange for Saber Intent Condensing Lotus Seeds.

This was because the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) in Song Shuhang’s hands was not the complete version.

Therefore, he decided to leave the fairy maiden some face and reluctantly gave her Saber Intent Condensing Lotus Seeds in exchange for the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique), which was of little significance to him.

As for Fairy Almighty Seller, she gave him two (Life Insurance Tickets) in order to complete the transaction.

These tickets were from the life insurance business that she and her master were starting up. When the owner of a ticker was faced with a major crisis, she and her master would use their spatial abilities to quickly look for the person in need of saving and save them.

Overall, both parties were satisfied with the transaction.

Fairy Almighty Seller took the batch of Saber Intent Condensing Lotus Seeds and left in satisfaction.

As for Song Shuhang, he happily stored the complete version of the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) and the two Life Insurance Tickets.

...When doing business, you should not easily let the other party know that you really wanted something, or else the other party could make use of that knowledge to take advantage of you.

This truth had been mentioned by Fairy Almighty Seller just a short while ago.

Song Shuhang felt that it made sense after listening to it, so he kept it in mind, and applied what he had learned.

Therefore, although he had wanted the complete version of the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) since the start, he took the initiative to show the first three styles of the (Inverted Scale Saber Technique) and his saber intent armor to Fairy Almighty Seller in order to lower the price. It looks like it really is effective! Fairy Almighty Seller gave me two tickets as a bonus!

The tickets were not actually very useful to Song Shuhang, as he had the Inner World and could directly escape into it should he face a dangerous situation. And if the Inner World was unreachable due to the space being sealed, then it was likely that Fairy Almighty Seller and the Almighty Merchant would not be able to get to him, either.

However, using this ticket as a gift to others was a pretty good use for them as well. Unfortunately, there are only two of them. Whom should I give these to?

“By the way, little friend Shuhang.” At this moment, Elder Sister White Dragon floated over and said softly, “Yu Jiaojiao should have sent you a full version of the (Divine Weapon Appraisal). You can take a look when you have time. However, since Slow-Witted Song had tinkered with it, don’t expect too much.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Thank you, Elder Sister White Dragon. By the way, is Sixteen awake?”

Elder Sister White Dragon smiled and said, “Mm-hm, she’s already awake. She should be out in a while.”

Song Shuhang took out his phone, clicked on the chat software, and then opened the chat between himself and Yu Jiaojiao. Soon, he found the <Divine Weapon Appraisal).

From its name, it seems like it’s a magical technique for appraising divine weapons?

Song Shuhang was very interested in what Slow-Witted Song researched. I wonder what tricks that guy found...

Upon closer inspection, the content had absolutely nothing to do with appraising divine weapons.

It was a small magical technique. A magical technique that could be used by a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm powerhouse.

Simply put, through this magical technique, a Tribulation Transcender could leave a rune mark on a magical treasure that only they could sense. After doing so, no matter where the magical treasure or item was thrown, it could instantly be summoned through the mark.

[With this little magical technique, my mother no longer has to worry about me losing things! -Slow-Witted Song.)

“...” Song Shuhang.

Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcenders are amazing, aren’t they?

A Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender can do whatever they want with their spatial abilities!

“A magical technique that’s completely useless.” Song Shuhang sighed. Behind him, the virtuous lamia pinched her chin thoughtfully.

After a while...

The virtuous lamia suddenly stretched out her hand, and slapped Song Shuhang’s treasured saber Broken Tyrant.

Pa

A small, snake-like rune mark was branded onto the treasured saber Broken Tyrant. “!!!” Song Shuhang’s eyes widened.

Isn’t this (Divine Weapon Appraisal) a magical technique that can only be used by Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcenders? Why is the virtuous lamia able to use it so easily?

The virtuous lamia had possessed strength at the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm back when she had been alive, but the issue was that her current self as a light of virtue did not have strength or abilities of the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm.

“Hehehehe.” The virtuous lamia waved her little hand proudly.

Nobody noticed that there was a Tribulation Bone flickering in the body of the virtuous fat whale underneath her tail.

During the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation, after the first tribulation wave, a Tribulation Transcender’s vitality could be birthed in one’s body, allowing the cultivator’s vitality to undergo humongous changes and break past its limit.

And after the second tribulation wave, the cultivator could instead condense a Tribulation Bone in their body. This wave was also known as the ‘spatial power ticket’. Normally, after the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage ended, the Tribulation Transcender would gain the ability to make contact with spatial forces thanks to the Tribulation Bone.

Song Shuhang had personally endured the second tribulation wave of the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation. However, as he, unfortunately, did not possess a cultivation of the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Realm, his body was not able to birth a Tribulation Bone.

“Fairy Waiting for a Promise, can you try summoning Broken Tyrant through the (Divine Weapon Appraisal)?” Nowadays, Song Shuhang was someone with a big heart, and he had become someone who was very accepting of things.

When it came to certain things that ordinary cultivators would find a hard time coming to terms with, he could very easily and quickly do

so.

Since some things already happened, one did not need to concern themself with the process as much as the result any longer-it was already a fact that the virtuous lamia could use the (Divine Weapon Appraisal), so there was no need to think about it any further. Anyhow, it was not like it was a bad thing.

The virtuous lamia posed like a bodybuilder, and then quickly nodded her head.

“Go!” Song Shuhang used the saber controlling technique, and sent the treasured saber Broken Tyrant into the sky. The treasured saber headed toward the other end of Heavenly Field Island. After doing this, Song Shuhang turned his head to look at the virtuous lamia.

The virtuous lamia began to summon the treasured saber Broken Tyrant according to the method recorded in the (Divine Weapon Appraisal).

However, while she could sense the distance between herself and the treasured saber, as well as its exact location on Heavenly Field Island, she could not summon it back to herself. It was because she did not have spatial abilities.

If one wanted to use spatial abilities, they were required to possess the Tribulation Bone, and they would need to transcend the Thousand Days Tribulation of the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation.

The virtuous lamia waved both of her hands, trying to cast the magical technique repeatedly, but nothing happened.

She turned her head stiffly, looking at Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang was thinking about how to comfort the virtuous lamia when there was suddenly a burst of mocking laughter from beside him... It was Fairy Creation.

She burst into laughter, and even began rolling on the floor as she laughed loudly.

She and the virtuous lamia were both partners and competitors.

The virtuous lamia was hit hard. She grabbed the tip of her tail while feeling aggrieved, and then rolled herself back into Song Shuhang’s body.

“Sure enough, one must not have their expectations set too high when it comes to cultivation techniques tinkered with by Slow-Witted Song. Eight out of ten times, things he tinkered with are trash he tossed away,” said Elder Sister White Dragon calmly. She had clearly suffered in the same manner in the past, which was why she was very vigilant toward anything that Slow-Witted Song had touched.

Song Shuhang said regretfully, “What a pity. If this (Divine Weapon Appraisal) really worked, it would be very useful.”

For example... In the middle of a fight, he could stamp a rune mark on the enemy’s magical treasure, and directly plunder it from them. Although it was very likely that the other party would immediately regain control and grab it back, if it happened out of nowhere and unexpectedly, it could affect the battle.

Another example was Senior Skylark’s bone of eternity: if she branded it with a mark, then she could easily retrieve it whenever she wanted.

Also, Senior White Two had been trying to capture the big-eyed planet for a while now. If he ever got the opportunity to stamp a mark on its body, then it would never be able to run from him, right?

Song Shuhang happily swam in a sea of his own thoughts.

Unfortunately, that was all that he could think about.

He stretched out his hand, made a hand seal, and prepared to use the saber controlling technique to summon back the treasured saber Broken Tyrant.

But suddenly, his hand paused-after the virtuous lamia rolled back into his body, the virtuous fat whale also rolled back into his body.

When the virtuous fat whale returned to his body, Song Shuhang suddenly felt something.

His consciousness was clearly able to lock on to the location of the treasured saber Broken Tyrant through a snake-shaped rune. At the same time, he got the feeling as if he could summon back the treasured saber Broken Tyrant by stretching out his hand.

So, Song Shuhang stretched out his hand, and started trying to grab at the air. Grab, grab, grab... “Shuhang, what are you doing?” Doudou looked at Song Shuhang, who looked like a fool at this moment.

“Huh?” Song Shuhang stopped grabbing at the air.

He fell into a state of contemplation. He felt that as long as he stretched out his hand, he would be able to retrieve the treasured saber Broken Tyrant, so why did it not come back? Was he lacking something? And so, he described what he felt just now to Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword and Elder Sister White Dragon. After listening, Elder Sister White Dragon smiled and said, “I get it... This (Divine Weapon Appraisal) is a magical technique similar to a spatial locator. For a Tribulation Transcender who possesses spatial abilities, as long as they have the coordinates, they can naturally retrieve their items through space.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword added, “But as you don’t have spatial abilities, then of course you can’t retrieve Broken Tyrant even if you have its coordinates.”

This was perhaps why the <Divine Weapon Appraisal) was a magical technique that could only be mastered by Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcenders—but for a Tribulation Transcender, this magical technique was quite useless.

Song Shuhang opened the (Divine Weapon Appraisal) sent by Yu Jiaojiao again and handed his phone over to Senior White. “In a while, I’ll add this (Divine Weapon Appraisal) to the group folder of the Nine Provinces Number One Group so that any interested seniors can take a look.”

Pa

A pure white crescent mark appeared on the back of Song Shuhang’s phone, and quickly disappeared. It had become a rune mark that only Senior White’s clone could see.

This time, Song Shuhang was not surprised or shocked at all.

A palm suddenly appeared in front of Song Shuhang, grabbing his phone and taking it away.

“The so-called method of ‘summoning a treasure’ is actually to snatch it back by hand...” Song Shuhang’s mouth twitched.

This completely ruined the images he had conjured in his mind just a short while ago.

How am I supposed to use such a move to snatch my enemy’s weapon?

As soon as my palm reaches out to grab the weapon, the enemy can just attack my palm.

“This magical technique is quite interesting.” After thinking about it, Senior White said, “Shuhang, to a certain extent, you can be considered to possess spatial abilities.”

Is Senior White referring to the Inner World?

“Just try it. It’s not like it costs you any money.” Senior White’s clone threw the phone back to Song Shuhang. Song Shuhang caught the phone, nodded, and then tried sensing the snake-shaped rune mark on the treasured saber Broken Tyrant.

After sensing Broken Tyrant, he felt as if he could retrieve it simply by grabbing at the air.

Doudou could not help but exclaim, “Woof!”

He tried using the same method he would use when opening the Inner World for his main body or with his clone.

Both his clone and his main body possessed the authority and ability to open the Inner World, so as long as they cooperated with one another, they could complete a positional exchange through the Inner World.

Now, what he was trying to do was go a step further and create two openings in the Inner World at the same time.

Song Shuhang asked, “Do you mean like last time?”

Did something go wrong? Did the spear that Pavilion Master Chu throw out accidentally penetrate through a fellow daoist who was flying on their sword?

The spear she threw out just now was actually aimed at that guy who had been hiding and peeping at them. Originally, she was planning on hitting the other party with the spear, and then dragging them back using spatial abilities.

Unexpectedly, the other party managed to escape using some tricks of their own. Song Shuhang pondered for a moment. He then stretched out his hand and touched the blood on the spear gently. Once his hand touched the blood, he activated the secret appraisal technique.

If it was really an enemy, then I should check who they are first... The price for the appraisal was minimal, only inflicting a small wound on him as the price. Song Shuhang did not even react to pain of this level.

[Mixed blood: This blood is a mixture of the blood of spirit beasts, fierce beasts, and humankind. With the help of this secret technique, a blood demonic god pillar can be summoned, and by making use of the demonic god energy in the demonic god pillar, a blood incarnation can be condensed. Once this incarnation receives a fatal attack, it will disappear.)

Those disciples in these realms aren’t qualified to leave their sects or forces yet, and once a cultivator does have the qualification to go and explore, they usually aren’t young anymore. Moreover, at that time, those disciples definitely wouldn’t stay as an ordinary university student and take classes for that long. At most, they would experience it for a short while, and then leave.”

Song Shuhang said, “That’s reasonable.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen said, “But in a while, I can change my identity and experience campus life with you.”

The corners of Song Shuhang’s mouth rose, and then he replied, “Okay.”

He also felt that he would enjoy such an experience with Sixteen.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “They’re here.”

In the sky above the university town, spatial fluctuations emerged.

Song Shuhang stood up. He then reached out and put on a hat on Sixteen’s head to hide her two beautiful little dragon horns.

In midair, a spatial gate opened.

Fairy Blue Phoenix and two young girls emerged from the void one after the other.

“Let’s go, Sixteen.” Song Shuhang summoned the Divine Lobster’s Chariot, and then stretched his hand out to Sixteen.

Su Clan’s Sixteen took Song Shuhang’s hand into hers, and let herself be pulled into the chariot.

The golden chariot rushed up toward the sky.

At the same time, Fairy Blue Phoenix also saw Song Shuhang and greeted them.

The two young girls following Fairy Blue Phoenix were carrying a large box in each of their arms.

Song Shuhang could sense from a distance that the two boxes in the hands of the two girls were exuding pure spiritual energy fluctuations.

Chapter 1900 Finally rid of poverty and rich

Fairy Blue Phoenix and Song Shuhang did not waste any time as the Beast Realm was currently in a very bad state, and they did not have much time to spare. Fairy Blue Phoenix landed on the Divine Lobster’s Chariot with the two young girls.

Immediately, they proceeded with the transaction.

Song Shuhang took out the small box that was given to him by Senior White Two, and handed it over to Fairy Blue Phoenix. “Fairy, inside this box is the method to deal with the Netherworld Evil Energy Infection plaguing the Beast Realm. It contains the recipe for a medicinal liquid. At present, this medicinal liquid cannot completely cure the evil energy infection, and it can only suppress and relieve symptoms. It will be more effective if you use it along with the method in the box. You can use this for now, and I should be able to provide you with a second, improved version of the medicinal liquid in the future. Once I have the recipe for it, I will immediately let you know.”

“Thank you, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.” Fairy Blue Phoenix carefully took the small box and opened it. Inside the box was a set of medicinal liquids and two booklets. One of these booklets was the recipe for the medicinal liquid, while the other was the plan to deal with the infection.

When her fingers touched the medicinal liquid, she sensed a kind of domineering power in the medicinal liquid. It could directly suppress the evil energy of the Netherworld.

What shocked her even more was that the words in the two booklets felt as if they were burning. As she looked at the words in the booklets, it felt as if she were staring straight at a perpetually burning sun.

It was immediately apparent to her that an Immortal had written the content of the two booklets. This increased their value to the extreme.

Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song actually went to an Immortal to ask for help for the Beast Realm.

It appears that the favor I owe him is much greater than I initially expected.

“Thank you.” She blushed slightly and thanked Song Shuhang again.

Song Shuhang laughed, and said, “You’re welcome. We’re both getting what we want here anyway.”

eV

Fairy Blue Phoenix smiled and gently placed the small box into a spatial magical treasure.

Afterward, she took out a scroll from her bosom, and handed it to Song Shuhang. “This is the (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique) that can be practiced all the way to the Ninth Stage. As for the last chapter to this technique, I’ll be sure to contact you when the Holy Mountain opens once more. When the time comes, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song can go and comprehend the technique over at the Holy Mountain.”

“I’ve really troubled you, Fairy.” Song Shuhang reached out and took the scroll.

At the side, Sixteen glanced over at Fairy Blue Phoenix’s chest—to have been able to hide such a large scroll there, it appeared that the creatures of the Beast Realm had much stronger physical qualities than humans. Should they be of the same realm, then it was likely that the people of the Beast Realm would completely outmatch them in terms of physique.

Even the two young ladies behind Fairy Blue Phoenix, while obviously young, were already about to catch up to Soft Feather in terms of chest size. It was truly enviable.

“In addition, we’ve prepared some small things for Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.” Fairy Blue Phoenix took the box that Yan was holding, and gave it to Song Shuhang. “Since Fellow Daoist said that the more normal the item, the better, we brought some things that we believe will fit your request. Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, see if you like it.”

“I’m an ordinary person, and what I pursue is ordinary things. The more commonplace it is, the better.” Song Shuhang laughed, took the box, and opened it. Sixteen leaned over to take a look.

After doing so, she saw that the box was filled with medicinal pills the size of beans. This box also possessed an effect similar to a spatial magical treasure. This one box of medicinal pills actually had a five-square-meter room worth of medicinal pills!

It should take several years to finish them if one were to consume one pill a day.

It isn’t spirit stones. Su Clan’s Sixteen chuckled to herself.

Smiling, Fairy Blue Phoenix said, “These are ape dragon pills required for the practice of the (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique). Taking a few pills before you practice will greatly increase the efficiency. In addition, taking one pill before a battle will also allow the (Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique) to perform much better. This medicinal pill is very easy to get in the Beast Realm, but as Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song is not from the Beast Realm, I thought that this should very much fit Fellow Daoist’s needs.”

“Good stuff.” Song Shuhang happily put away the box.

Although it wasn’t spirit stones, the medicine pills in the box were better than spirit stones for him.

“It’s great that Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song is satisfied,” said Fairy Blue Phoenix—to be honest, even if he only asked for common things, trying to satisfy Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song as much as possible was a lot more of a headache than preparing great treasures.

She then turned around, took the box from Ling, and handed the box over to Song Shuhang. “This is the second gift we prepared for Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.”

What is it going to be this time?

Song Shuhang took the box and opened it.

When he opened the box, its contents reflected the sunlight and emitted a colorful light. The items in the box had an extremely pure aura and a gem-like light.

It’s spirit stones!!

Song Shuhang was overjoyed.

I’ve finally rid myself of poverty and become rich!

From this moment on, Song “Penniless” Shuhang is a thing of the past. Now, please call me Song “Has a Box Full of Spirit Stones” Shuhang

At this moment, Fairy Blue Phoenix introduced the items inside the box. “This is a treasure unique to our Beast Realm. They’re seeds for gemstone fruit.”

What?

They’re seeds?

Not spirit stones?

Song Shuhang looked confused.

Sixteen held back her smile. After all, she wanted to give Song Shuhang face in front of outsiders, so she couldn’t just pull the rug from under his feet right now.

Fairy Blue Phoenix explained softly, “The gemstone fruit is an immortal fruit with an exceptional taste. It is easy to grow, and possesses strong resistance and endurance. As long as it is given sufficient spiritual energy, it can grow rapidly. The more abundant the spiritual energy, the faster it will grow. If it is planted in a spiritual vein, it could germinate, grow, and bear fruit in a few breaths of time. Other than having an exceptional taste, its fruit has a series of effects such as prolonging life, enhancing cultivation, and restoring spiritual energy. Immortal Fairy Bie Xue once purchased a batch of it after contacting us. I believe that this is perfect for Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.”

Song Shuhang held up one of the seeds, which looked exactly like a spirit stone. The spiritual energy contained in it could seemingly be absorbed directly.

As if she could read Song Shuhang’s thoughts, Fairy Blue Phoenix added, “The gemstone fruit seeds we provided you were specially picked and cultivated. Each of these seeds is as beautiful as a spirit stone. In fact, they are just like spirit stones, and the spiritual energy inside them can be directly extracted for a cultivator to use. Of course, using them in such a way is considered crude.”

“Good stuff.” Song Shuhang laughed and put away the seeds in the box.

Well, at the very least, he could plant the seeds in his Inner World.

“Finally, we prepared one more gift.” Fairy Blue Phoenix reached out and stroked her hair. After that, eight bee-sized light clusters appeared in the palm of her hand.

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “What’s this?”

Fairy Blue Phoenix introduced it with a blushing face. “These are little monster beasts that live with us blue phoenixes. We usually call them 0. They can help Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song plant the gemstone fruits seeds and take care of the growth of the fruit trees. Moreover, when the gemstone fruits blossom, they can help spread the pollen and create a virtuous cycle. In addition, if there are any other flowers or fruit-like spirit plants where Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song plans to grow the gemstone fruit trees, they can also collect nectar like bees.”

“Wonderful.” Song Shuhang smiled and took the eight little clusters of light—these were exactly what he currently needed.
